                                              EXTERNAL SYMBOL DICTIONARY                                     PAGE    1
 SYMBOL  TYPE ID  ADDR  LENGTH LD ID
 
 
FIXTOS    SD  01 001800 001224
IJFUZZZZ  ER  02

       PATCH TOS DISTRIBUTION SYSRES                                                                           PAGE    1
 
 
  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                            TOS CL2-5 09/07/75
 
                                      2          PRINT NOGEN
001800                                3 FIXTOS   START X'1800'
000008                                4 R8       EQU   8
000009                                5 R9       EQU   9
00000C                                6 R12      EQU   12
001800 05C0                           7          BALR  R12,0
001802                                8          USING *,R12
                                      9          OPEN  OLDTOS,NEWTOS
001816 4580 C106            01908    18          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY IPL,SUPVR(F1)
00181A 4190 0057            00057    19          LA    R9,87           COPY 87 RECORDS IN CIL
00181E 4580 C0E8            018EA    20          BAL   R8,COPYRECS
                                     21          GET   OLDTOS          READ $$BCMT06(REC88)
                                     26 * THIS TRANSIENT CLOSES TAPE WORK FILES FOR DTFMT.
                                     27 * IT WRITES A TAPEMARK ON AND REWINDS THE TAPE.
                                     28 * THE FIRST CCW IN THE CHAIN WAS APPARENTLY INTENDED AS A MODESET,
                                     29 * MAYBE TO CHANGE THE DENSITY, BUT USES A COMMAND CODE OF X'F3'.
                                     30 * ACCORDING TO THE 2803 MANUAL THIS IS AN INVALID COMMAND CODE
                                     31 * AND SHOULD RAISE AN EXCEPTION AS HERCULES DOES.  IT'S HARD TO
                                     32 * BELIEVE THAT THIS VERSION OF TOS WAS RELEASED WITH THIS BUG AS NO
                                     33 * ASSEMBLIES OR COMPILES (EXCEPT FORTRAN) WOULD WORK CORRECTLY.
                                     34 * PERHAPS THE BUG WAS IN THE 2803 WHICH IGNORED AN INVALID CODE INSTEAD
                                     35 * OF RAISING AN EXCEPTION. SO LET'S INCREASE THE CCW ADDR. IN THE CCB
                                     36 * BY 8 TO THE NEXT CCW IN THE CHAIN, AND NOT USE THE BAD MODESET CCW.
                                     37 * VER X'E8'
                                     38 * REP X'F0'
00182E 95E8 C305      01B07          39          CLI   IOAREA+227,X'E8'
001832 4770 C0DA            018DC    40          BNE   CANCEL
001836 92F0 C305      01B07          41          MVI   IOAREA+227,X'F0'
                                     42          PUT   NEWTOS
001846 4580 C106            01908    47          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY REST OF CIL(F2)
00184A 4190 023A            0023A    48          LA    R9,570          COPY 570 RECORDS IN RL
00184E 4580 C0E8            018EA    49          BAL   R8,COPYRECS
                                     50          GET   OLDTOS          READ IJALE3(REC571)
                                     55 *                             (PHASE($LNKEDTH),CSECT(IJALRD27))
                                     56 * THE LINKAGE EDITOR WILL CANCEL IF SYSLST IS ASSIGNED TO TAPE.
                                     57 * AT ONE POINT IT DOES NOT MODIFY ITSELF TO ALLOW FOR TAPE AND STILL
                                     58 * USES A PRINTER CCW CODE INSTEAD OF CHANGING IT TO A TAPE CCW CODE.
                                     59 * IT TRIES TO PRINT A BLANK LINE AFTER THE LINK EDIT MAP AND BEFORE
                                     60 * THE LISTING OF PHASES.  WE CAN PATCH IT TO BRANCH AROUND THE PRINTING
                                     61 * OF THE BLANK LINE.  IF IMPLEMENTED THE BLANK LINE WILL ALSO NO LONGER
                                     62 * BE THERE IF WE ARE GOING DIRECTLY TO A PRINTER.  IF YOU WANT TO
                                     63 * IMPLEMENT THIS FIX REMOVE THE ASTERISK IN COL.1 IN THE NEXT 3 LINES.
                                     64 *    CLC IOAREA+28(4),=X'4110E6C6'
                                     65 *    BNE CANCEL
                                     66 *    MVC IOAREA+28(4),=X'47F0E600'
                                     67          PUT   NEWTOS
00186A 4890 C166            01968    72          LH    R9,=H'7773'     COPY 7773 MORE RECORDS IN RL
00186E 4580 C0E8            018EA    73          BAL   R8,COPYRECS
                                     74          GET   OLDTOS          READ IJVTE210(REC8345)
                                     79 *                             (PHASE(ATLEFE2),CSECT(IJVTE222))
                                     80 * AUTOTEST GETS STUCK IN A LOOP WAITING FOR CUE (CONTROL UNIT END)

       PATCH TOS DISTRIBUTION SYSRES                                                                           PAGE    2
 
 
  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                            TOS CL2-5 09/07/75
 
                                     81 * WHEN THERE IS UE (UNIT EXCEPTION, TAPE MARK); WE NEVER GET THE CUE.
                                     82 * THE GENERALIZED I/O ROUTINE IS CODED--
                                     83 *     DO EXCP,WAIT
                                     84 *      TM    CCB+4,X'01'  WAS THERE UE (TAPE MARK) IN CSW
                                     85 *      BCR   8,R8 BZ        NO, CONTINUE NORMALLY
                                     86 *      TM    CCB+4,X'20'    YES, WAS THERE CUE (WAS IT CONTROL OP?)
                                     87 *      BCR   1,R8 BO          YES, CONTINUE NORMALLY (FSR,BSR?)
                                     88 *     AT THIS POINT THERE WAS NO CUE, SO IT MUST HAVE BEEN A READ,
                                     89 *     THEN DO THE END-OF-FILE ROUTINE EXCEPT IT WAS REALLY THE RESULT
                                     90 *     OF A BSR OPERATION SO IT GETS CONFUSED.
                                     91 * IF THERE IS NO TAPEMARK, EVERYTHING IS OK AND CONTINUE NORMALLY
                                     92 * IF THERE IS A TAPEMARK THIS COULD MEAN AN END-OF-FILE ON A READ OR
                                     93 * IT COULD MEAN A TAPEMARK WAS SENSED ON A FSR OR BSR CONTROL COMMAND,
                                     94 * I.E., DID WE GET UE(TM) AS A RESULT OF CONTROL OP (BSR,FSR) OR WAS
                                     95 * IT A READ?  IT LOOKS LIKE IT'S USING THE CUE TO DETERMINE IF THE UE
                                     96 * WAS THE RESULT OF A CONTROL OPERATION LIKE BSR AND FSR.
                                     97 * I CAN'T FIND ANYTHING IN THE PRINCIPLES OF OPERATION OR THE
                                     98 * 2803 MANUAL THAT SAYS CONTROL UNIT END IS PRESENTED BECAUSE THE
                                     99 * OPERATION IS FSR OR BSR.  IT SEEMS TO SAY THAT CUE WILL ONLY OCCUR
                                    100 * AFTER AN OPERATION WAS NOT STARTED BECAUSE THE CONTROL UNIT WAS BUSY
                                    101 * AND PERHAPS ONLY ON DEVICES SHARING A CONTROL UNIT.
                                    102 * SO WE NEVER GET THE CUE ON THE BSR AND FSR.
                                    103 * THERE ARE DIFFERENT WAYS OF CHANGING THE TEST FOR CONTROL OP.
                                    104 * LET'S CHANGE THE TEST TO INSTEAD LOOK AT THE CCW COMMAND CODE.
                                    105 * CHECK LAST 2 BITS OF CCW COMMAND CODE, IF BOTH ON IT IS CONTROL OP.
                                    106 * VER X'9120F4A6' IS IT CUE (CONTROL OP?)
                                    107 * REP X'9103F4B2' IS IT A CCW CONTROL OPERATION
00187E D503 C23A C15E 01A3C 01960   108          CLC   IOAREA+24(4),=X'9120F4A6' TM CCB+4,X'20' CUE IN CSW?
001884 4770 C0DA            018DC   109          BNE   CANCEL
001888 D203 C23A C162 01A3C 01964   110          MVC   IOAREA+24(4),=X'9103F4B2' TM CCW,X'03'   CTRL.OP.?
                                    111          PUT   NEWTOS
00189A 4580 C106            01908   116          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY REST OF RL(F3)
00189E 4580 C106            01908   117          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY SD(F4)
0018A2 4580 C106            01908   118          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY SL-ASSEMBLY(F5)
0018A6 4580 C106            01908   119          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY SL-COBOL(F6)
0018AA 4580 C106            01908   120          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY EOV(F7)
0018AE 4580 C106            01908   121          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY PID RECORDS(F8)
0018B2 4580 C106            01908   122          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY LIB.DIST.(F9)
0018B6 4580 C106            01908   123          BAL   R8,COPYFILE     COPY PID RECORD(F10)
                                    124          CNTRL NEWTOS,BSF      BACKUP PAST TAPE MARK
                                    130          CLOSE OLDTOS,NEWTOS   WRITE TWO TAPE MARKS
                                    139          EOJ
                                    142 CANCEL   PDUMP IOAREA,IOAREA+4096
                                    147          CANCEL
                                    151 COPYRECS GET   OLDTOS
                                    156          PUT   NEWTOS
001902 4690 C0E8            018EA   161          BCT   R9,COPYRECS
001906 07F8                         162          BR    R8
                                    163 COPYFILE GET   OLDTOS
                                    168          PUT   NEWTOS
001920 47F0 C106            01908   173          B     COPYFILE

       PATCH TOS DISTRIBUTION SYSRES                                                                           PAGE    3

// EXEC TPTP
 

 
// UTT TF,FF,A=(81,81),B=(80,80),IR,OR
// FS 2,80,1
// END
TAPE TO TAPE UTILITY
INPUT RECORD LENGTH 0081
OUTPUT RECORD LENGTH  0080
INPUT BLOCK LENGTH 00081
OUTPUT BLOCK LENGTH 00080
INPUT OPTION REWIND
OUTPUT OPTION    REWIND         ,WRITE TAPE MARK
2 INPUT,2 OUTPUT AREAS ASSIGNED
RECORD FORMAT FIXED
TYPE FIELD SELECT
STARTING RECORD NUMBER  00000001
8001D IS IT 
REPLY Y
NUMBER OF INPUT BLOCKS PROCESSED  000015
NUMBER OF OUTPUT BLOCKS PROCESSED 000015
END OF JOB

// JOB DEMOCOBD SAMPLE COBOL PROGRAM                                    00.00.00
// OPTION LINK,SYM,LISTX
// EXEC COBOL
 
CBL DMAP=21A0,PMAP=21A0

       LINE NO. SEQ. NO.          SOURCE STATEMENT                                                    CBT CL2-6 09/07/75
 
             1          IDENTIFICATION DIVISION.
             2          PROGRAM-ID. 'SAMPLE'.
             3          AUTHOR. A PROGRAMMER.
             4          REMARKS. THIS IS A SAMPLE COBOL (D LEVEL) PROGRAM FOR A TYPICAL
             5              BUSINESS REPORT.  IT ALSO DEMONSTRATES A CONTROL BREAK,
             6              A BINARY SEARCH FOR A TABLE, CALLING A SUBROUTINE,
             7              AND USES BOTH A LINE COUNTER AND THE COBOL USE OF CH.12
             8              ON THE PRINTER CARRIAGE TAPE.
             9
            10              THIS PROGRAM IS INTENDED TO SHOW AN EARLY 1968 PROGRAM
            11              AND THEREFORE BEFORE PROFESSOR DIJKSTRA'S LETTER ON 'GOTO'
            12              STATEMENTS WAS PUBLISHED BY THE ACM, I.E. BEFORE THE DAYS
            13              OF STRUCTURED PROGRAMMING.  'GO TO' VERBS ARE USED
            14              IN THE PROGRAM AS NECESSARY AND CORRECTLY AS IN
            15              THE METHODS OF 'MODULAR PROGRAMMING'.
            16
            17              THE ONLY WAY OF INCLUDING COMMENTS IN THIS VERSION OF COBOL
            18              IS THIS 'REMARKS' PARAGRAPH AND A 'NOTE' VERB AS USED IN THE
            19              PROCEDURE DIVISION.   EVERYTHING FROM 'NOTE' TO THE END OF
            20              THE SENTENCE (PERIOD) IS A COMMENT.  IF THE 'NOTE' IS THE
            21              FIRST VERB IN A PARAGRAPH THE WHOLE PARAGRAPH IS A COMMENT.
            22              AN ASTERISK IN COL. 7 IS IGNORED AND DOES NOT MEAN A COMMENT.
            23
            24              THE 'DMAP' AND 'PMAP' OPTIONS ON THE 'CBL' OPTION CARD ONLY
            25              AFFECT THE SOURCE CODE LISTING.  IF YOU KNOW THE ACTUAL
            26              LINKEDIT ADDRESS THEY CAN BE USED AS AN OFFSET TO SHOW
            27              ACTUAL CORE LOCATIONS ON THE SOURCE CODE LISTING FOR
            28              THE DATA MAP (SYM) AND PROCEDURE MAP (LISTX) TO AID
            29              IN DEBUGGING.
            30
            31              THIS PROGRAM SHOWS THE PRINTING METHOD OF SETTING UP
            32              ALL LINES IN WORKING STORAGE AND THEN USING THE 'FROM'
            33              OPTION ON THE 'WRITE' TO SEND EACH ONE TO THE PRINTER.
            34
            35          ENVIRONMENT DIVISION.
            36          CONFIGURATION SECTION.
            37          SOURCE-COMPUTER. IBM-360.
            38          OBJECT-COMPUTER. IBM-360.
            39          INPUT-OUTPUT SECTION.
            40          FILE-CONTROL.
            41              SELECT PAY-FILE   ASSIGN TO 'SYS007' UNIT-RECORD 2501.
            42              SELECT PRINT-FILE ASSIGN TO 'SYS009' UNIT-RECORD 1403.
            43          I-O-CONTROL.
            44              APPLY EOP TO FORM-OVERFLOW ON PRINT-FILE.
            45
            46          DATA DIVISION.
            47          FILE SECTION.
            48          FD  PAY-FILE
            49              LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED
            50              RECORDING MODE IS F
            51              RECORD CONTAINS 75 CHARACTERS
            52              DATA RECORD IS EMPLOYEE-RECORD.

            54              05  EM-DEPARTMENT       PICTURE XX.

            72          WORKING-STORAGE SECTION.

            78              02  FILLER   COMPUTATIONAL-3.

            85                  05  WS-DT-FIT-WITH  PICTURE S9(5)V99    VALUE ZERO.
            86                  05  WS-DT-SIT-WITH  PICTURE S9(5)V99    VALUE ZERO.

            91                  05  WS-FT-SIT-WITH  PICTURE S9(7)V99    VALUE ZERO.
            92                  05  WS-FT-OTH-DED   PICTURE S9(7)V99    VALUE ZERO.
            93                  05  WS-FT-NET-PAY   PICTURE S9(7)V99    VALUE ZERO.
            94              02  FILLER.
            95                  05  ASA             PICTURE X           VALUE SPACE.
            96                  05  WS-DEPARTMENT   PICTURE XX.
            97                  05  DEPTS-TABLE.
            98                      10  FILLER      PICTURE X(12) VALUE '10     SALES'.
            99                      10  FILLER      PICTURE X(12) VALUE '20      MFG.'.
           100                      10  FILLER      PICTURE X(12) VALUE '30  BUSINESS'.
           101                      10  FILLER      PICTURE X(12) VALUE '40    TRANS.'.
           102                      10  FILLER      PICTURE X(12) VALUE '50 ENGINEER.'.
           103                  05  DEPT-TABLE REDEFINES DEPTS-TABLE OCCURS 5 TIMES.
           104                      10  DEPT-CODE   PICTURE XX.
           105                      10  DEPT-DESC   PICTURE X(10).
           106              02  BLANK-LINE          PICTURE X           VALUE SPACE.
           107              02  HEADING1.
           108                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X.
           109                  05  H1-TODAY        PICTURE X(8).
           110                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(40)       VALUE SPACES.

           111                  05  FILLER PICTURE X(70) VALUE 'COBOL-D SAMPLE PROGRAM'.
           112                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE 'PAGE '.
           113                  05  H1-PAGE         PICTURE ZZ9.
           114              02  HEADING2.
           115                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(14) VALUE ' DEPT.    NAME'.
           116                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(15)       VALUE SPACES.
           117                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(100)      VALUE
           118                         'SOC.SEC.NO.        SALARY         F.I.T.
           119         -               'S.I.T.          OTHER           NET'.
           120              02  UNDER-LINE.
           121                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(14) VALUE ' _____    ____'.
           122                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(15)       VALUE SPACES.
           123                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(100)      VALUE
           124                         '___________        ______         ______
           125         -               '______          _____           ___'.
           126              02  DETAIL-LINE.
           127                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X           VALUE SPACE.
           128                  05  DL-DEPARTMENT   PICTURE XX.
           129                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(4)        VALUE SPACES.
           130                  05  DL-NAME         PICTURE X(20).
           131                  05  FILLER          PICTURE XX          VALUE SPACES.
           132                  05  DL-SSN13        PICTURE XXX.
           133                  05  DL-SSN-HYP1     PICTURE X.
           134                  05  DL-SSN45        PICTURE XX.
           135                  05  DL-SSN-HYP2     PICTURE X.
           136                  05  DL-SSN69        PICTURE XXXX.
           137                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           138                  05  DL-SALARY       PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           139                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           140                  05  DL-FIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           141                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           142                  05  DL-SIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           143                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           144                  05  DL-OTH-DED      PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           145                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           146                  05  DL-NET-PAY      PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           147              02  ERROR-LINE.
           148                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X           VALUE SPACE.
           149                  05  EL-DEPARTMENT   PICTURE XX.
           150                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(4)        VALUE SPACES.
           151                  05  EL-NAME         PICTURE X(20).
           152                  05  FILLER          PICTURE XX          VALUE SPACES.
           153                  05  EL-SSN13        PICTURE XXX.
           154                  05  EL-SSN-HYP1     PICTURE X.
           155                  05  EL-SSN45        PICTURE XX.
           156                  05  EL-SSN-HYP2     PICTURE X.
           157                  05  EL-SSN69        PICTURE XXXX.
           158                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           159                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(13) VALUE 'ERROR IN DATA'.
           160              02  DEPARTMENT-LINE.
           161                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(12)       VALUE SPACES.
           162                  05  DT-DEPT-DESC    PICTURE X(10)       VALUE SPACES.
           163                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(12) VALUE ' DEPARTMENT'.
           164                  05  DT-DEPARTMENT   PICTURE X(2).
           165                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(9)     VALUE ' TOTALS'.
           166                  05  DT-SALARY       PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.

           167                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           168                  05  DT-FIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           169                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           170                  05  DT-SIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           171                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           172                  05  DT-OTH-DED      PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           173                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(5)        VALUE SPACES.
           174                  05  DT-NET-PAY      PICTURE ZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           175                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X           VALUE '*'.
           176              02  FINAL-TOTAL-LINE.
           177                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(28)       VALUE SPACES.
           178                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(15)  VALUE 'FINAL TOTALS'.
           179                  05  FT-SALARY       PICTURE ZZZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           180                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(3)        VALUE SPACES.
           181                  05  FT-FIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           182                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(3)        VALUE SPACES.
           183                  05  FT-SIT-WITH     PICTURE ZZZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           184                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(3)        VALUE SPACES.
           185                  05  FT-OTH-DED      PICTURE ZZZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           186                  05  FILLER          PICTURE X(3)        VALUE SPACES.
           187                  05  FT-NET-PAY      PICTURE ZZZZ,ZZZ.99-.
           188                  05  FILLER          PICTURE XX          VALUE '**'.
           189
           190          PROCEDURE DIVISION.
           191              NOTE THE REQUIREMENT OF THE 'ENTER' VERBS WHEN CALLING
           192                  A SUBROUTINE.  NOTE WE ARE USING A CONTROL BREAK
           193                  SO WE READ THE FIRST RECORD IN HOUSEKEEPING.
           194              OPEN INPUT PAY-FILE, OUTPUT PRINT-FILE.
           195              ENTER LINKAGE.
           196              CALL 'GETDATE' USING H1-TODAY.
           197              ENTER COBOL.
           198              PERFORM HEADING-ROUTINE THRU HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
           199              READ PAY-FILE AT END GO TO END-OF-JOB.
           200              MOVE EM-DEPARTMENT TO WS-DEPARTMENT.
           201          MAIN-LOOP.
           202              IF EOP OR LINE-CNTR > 56
           203                  PERFORM HEADING-ROUTINE THRU HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
           204              EXAMINE EM-SALARY-X  REPLACING LEADING SPACES BY ZEROS.
           205              EXAMINE EM-OTH-DED-X REPLACING LEADING SPACES BY ZEROS.
           206              IF EM-SALARY IS NUMERIC AND EM-OTH-DED IS NUMERIC
           207                       PERFORM DATA-IS-GOOD THRU DATA-IS-GOOD-EXIT
           208                  ELSE PERFORM DATA-IS-BAD  THRU DATA-IS-BAD-EXIT.
           209              READ PAY-FILE AT END GO TO END-OF-JOB.
           210              IF EM-DEPARTMENT NOT = WS-DEPARTMENT
           211                  PERFORM DEPARTMENT-TOTAL THRU DEPARTMENT-TOTAL-EXIT.
           212              GO TO MAIN-LOOP.
           213          END-OF-JOB.
           214              PERFORM FINAL-TOTALS THRU FINAL-TOTALS-EXIT.
           215              CLOSE PAY-FILE, PRINT-FILE.
           216              STOP RUN.
           217
           218          HEADING-ROUTINE.
           219              ADD 1 TO WS-PAGE
           220              MOVE WS-PAGE TO H1-PAGE
           221              NOTE THAT 'AFTER ADVANCING 0' MEANS SKIP TO A NEW PAGE,
           222                  AND 'AFTER ADVANCING NAME' WOULD NEED TO BE A VALID

           223                  ASA CHARACTER.
           224              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM HEADING1 AFTER ADVANCING 0
           225              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM HEADING2 AFTER ADVANCING 2
           226              MOVE '+' TO ASA
           227              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM UNDER-LINE AFTER ADVANCING ASA
           228              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM BLANK-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1
           229              MOVE 4 TO LINE-CNTR.
           230          HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
           231              EXIT.
           232
           233          DATA-IS-GOOD.
           234              MULTIPLY EM-SALARY BY .14  GIVING WS-FIT-WITH ROUNDED
           235              MULTIPLY EM-SALARY BY .025 GIVING WS-SIT-WITH ROUNDED
           236              COMPUTE WS-NET-PAY = EM-SALARY - WS-FIT-WITH - WS-SIT-WITH -
           237                  EM-OTH-DED
           238              ADD EM-SALARY      TO WS-DT-SALARY
           239              ADD WS-FIT-WITH    TO WS-DT-FIT-WITH
           240              ADD WS-SIT-WITH    TO WS-DT-SIT-WITH
           241              ADD EM-OTH-DED     TO WS-DT-OTH-DED
           242              ADD WS-NET-PAY     TO WS-DT-NET-PAY
           243              MOVE EM-DEPARTMENT TO DL-DEPARTMENT
           244              MOVE EM-NAME       TO DL-NAME
           245              MOVE EM-SSN13      TO DL-SSN13
           246              MOVE EM-SSN45      TO DL-SSN45
           247              MOVE EM-SSN69      TO DL-SSN69
           248              MOVE '-'           TO DL-SSN-HYP1, DL-SSN-HYP2
           249              MOVE EM-SALARY     TO DL-SALARY
           250              MOVE WS-FIT-WITH   TO DL-FIT-WITH
           251              MOVE WS-SIT-WITH   TO DL-SIT-WITH
           252              MOVE EM-OTH-DED    TO DL-OTH-DED
           253              MOVE WS-NET-PAY    TO DL-NET-PAY
           254              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM DETAIL-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1
           255              ADD 1 TO LINE-CNTR.
           256          DATA-IS-GOOD-EXIT.
           257              EXIT.
           258          DATA-IS-BAD.
           259              MOVE EM-DEPARTMENT TO EL-DEPARTMENT
           260              MOVE EM-NAME       TO EL-NAME
           261              MOVE EM-SSN13      TO EL-SSN13
           262              MOVE EM-SSN45      TO EL-SSN45
           263              MOVE EM-SSN69      TO EL-SSN69
           264              MOVE '-'           TO EL-SSN-HYP1, EL-SSN-HYP2
           265              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM ERROR-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1
           266              ADD 1 TO LINE-CNTR.
           267          DATA-IS-BAD-EXIT.
           268              EXIT.
           269
           270              NOTE THE CONTROL BREAK ROUTINE WILL CREATE AND PRINT
           271                  THE DEPARTMENT TOTAL LINE, ROLL THE DEPARTMENT TOTALS
           272                  TO FINAL TOTALS AND THEN CLEAR DEPARTMENT TOTALS.
           273          DEPARTMENT-TOTAL.
           274              MOVE WS-DEPARTMENT TO DT-DEPARTMENT
           275              NOTE WE USE A BINARY SEARCH TO GET A DEPARTMENT NAME.
           276              MOVE 6 TO UPPER-LIMIT.
           277              MOVE ZERO TO LOWER-LIMIT.
           278          DEPT-SEARCH.

           279              COMPUTE IDX = (UPPER-LIMIT + LOWER-LIMIT) / 2
           280              IF IDX = LOWER-LIMIT
           281                 GO TO DEPT-BAD.
           282              IF DEPT-CODE (IDX) LESS THAN WS-DEPARTMENT
           283                 MOVE IDX TO LOWER-LIMIT
           284                 GO TO DEPT-SEARCH.
           285              IF DEPT-CODE (IDX) GREATER THAN WS-DEPARTMENT
           286                 MOVE IDX TO UPPER-LIMIT
           287                 GO TO DEPT-SEARCH.
           288              MOVE DEPT-DESC (IDX) TO DT-DEPT-DESC
           289              GO TO DEPT-END-SEARCH.
           290          DEPT-BAD.
           291              MOVE 'UNKNOWN' TO DT-DEPT-DESC.
           292          DEPT-END-SEARCH.
           293              MOVE WS-DT-SALARY   TO DT-SALARY
           294              MOVE WS-DT-FIT-WITH TO DT-FIT-WITH
           295              MOVE WS-DT-SIT-WITH TO DT-SIT-WITH
           296              MOVE WS-DT-OTH-DED  TO DT-OTH-DED
           297              MOVE WS-DT-NET-PAY  TO DT-NET-PAY
           298              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM DEPARTMENT-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1
           299              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM BLANK-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1
           300              ADD 2 TO LINE-CNTR
           301              ADD WS-DT-SALARY   TO WS-FT-SALARY
           302              ADD WS-DT-FIT-WITH TO WS-FT-FIT-WITH
           303              ADD WS-DT-SIT-WITH TO WS-FT-SIT-WITH
           304              ADD WS-DT-OTH-DED  TO WS-FT-OTH-DED
           305              ADD WS-DT-NET-PAY  TO WS-FT-NET-PAY
           306              MOVE ZEROS TO WS-DT-SALARY, WS-DT-FIT-WITH, WS-DT-SIT-WITH,
           307                  WS-DT-OTH-DED, WS-DT-NET-PAY
           308              MOVE EM-DEPARTMENT TO WS-DEPARTMENT.
           309          DEPARTMENT-TOTAL-EXIT.
           310              EXIT.
           311
           312          FINAL-TOTALS.
           313              PERFORM DEPARTMENT-TOTAL THRU DEPARTMENT-TOTAL-EXIT
           314              MOVE WS-FT-SALARY   TO FT-SALARY
           315              MOVE WS-FT-FIT-WITH TO FT-FIT-WITH
           316              MOVE WS-FT-SIT-WITH TO FT-SIT-WITH
           317              MOVE WS-FT-OTH-DED  TO FT-OTH-DED
           318              MOVE WS-FT-NET-PAY  TO FT-NET-PAY
           319              WRITE PRINT-LINE FROM FINAL-TOTAL-LINE AFTER ADVANCING 1.
           320          FINAL-TOTALS-EXIT.
           321              EXIT.

// JOB DEMOPLI1 ECLIPTIC COORDINATE TABLE                               00.00.26
// OPTION LINK,SYM,LISTX
// EXEC PL/I
 

         TOS PL/I COMPILER  360M-PL-410 CL2-4              DEMOPLI1            09/07/75            PAGE 001


                                                    O P T I O N S  L I S T

* PROCESS STMT  (PRINT STATEMENT NUMBER IF ABEND)

OPTIONS TAKEN ARE LIST,LISTX,SYM,XREF,ERRS,48C,OPT,STMT.

         TOS PL/I COMPILER  360M-PL-410 CL2-4              DEMOPLI1            09/07/75            PAGE 002


 /* SAMPLE SCIENTIFIC ORIENTED PL/I PROGRAM */

                     /* SAMPLE SCIENTIFIC ORIENTED PL/I PROGRAM */
                     /* USES THE 48 CHARACTER SET SYMBOLS */
                     /* DEMONSTRATES STREAM ORIENTED I/O */
                     /*  LIST MODE-- */
                     /*   (FIELDS) */
                     /*    FIELDS WILL BE POSITIONED AT PRE-DETERMINED TAB STOPS WITH */
                     /*       BUILT IN FORMATTING DEPENDING ON FIELD TYPE */
                     /*    TAB STOPS CAN BE CHANGED BY ASSEMBLING THE IJKZL MACRO */
                     /*    TO MAKE PERMANENT CATALOG TO RELOCATABLE LIBRARY AS IJKTLTB */
                     /*    DEFAULT IS 'IJKZL (1,25,49,73,97,121,FF)' */
                     /*    DEFAULT IJKTLTB TABS ARE PRINT POSITIONS 1,25,49,73,97,121 */
                     /*  EDIT MODE-- */
                     /*   (FIELDS) (FORTRAN LIKE FORMAT CODES) */
     1               ECLIPT.. PROCEDURE OPTIONS(MAIN),.
     2                 DECLARE DATE BUILTIN,
                               TODAY CHAR(8) STATIC INIT ('  /  /  '),
                               PAGE FIXED DEC(3,0),
                               DECL (12),.
     3                 SUBSTR(TODAY,1,2) = SUBSTR(DATE,3,2),.
     4                 SUBSTR(TODAY,4,2) = SUBSTR(DATE,5,2),.
     5                 SUBSTR(TODAY,7,2) = SUBSTR(DATE,1,2),.
     6                 PAGE=1,.
     7                 PUT LIST (TODAY,'ECLIPTIC COORDINATE TABLE','PAGE',PAGE),.
     8                 PUT SKIP(3) EDIT ('0000     0005     0010     0015     0020     0025
                          0030     0035     0040     0045     0050     0055')
                           (COLUMN(16), A),.
     9                 PUT SKIP(2),.
    10                 DO I = 100 TO 2400 BY 100,.
    11                   RAH = (I-100) / 100,.
    12                   DO J = 1 TO 12,.
    13                     DECL(J)= SIND((RAH+(J-1)/12)*15)*23.445,.
    14                   END,.
    15                   PUT EDIT (I-100,DECL) (COLUMN(7), F(4), 12 F(9,2)),.
    16                 END,.
    17               END ECLIPT,.

         TOS PL/I COMPILER  360M-PL-410 CL2-4              DEMOPLI1            09/07/75            PAGE 003


                         S Y M B O L     T A B L E     L I S T I N G

 DATE                                 01 1 BUILTIN

 PAGE                            0103 01 1             ARITHM. DECIMAL FIXED  3,0  AUTOM. INT
 DECL                            0104 01 1 ARRAY       ARITHM. DECIMAL FLOAT   6   AUTOM. INT

// JOB DEMOGRPH PRINT GRAPH OF A FUNCTION                               00.00.40
// OPTION LINK,NOXREF
// EXEC FORTRAN
 

                               TAPE OPERATING SYSTEM/360 FORTRAN   360M-FO-409 CL 2-3

          C  SAMPLE PROGRAM IN BASIC FORTRAN IV
          C  GRAPH - PRINT THE GRAPH OF A FUNCTION
          C    PRINT ONE GRAPH ON AN 14 7/8" X 11" PIECE OF PAPER AT 8LPI
          C  DEMONSTRATES THE USE OF COMMON FOR A GLOBAL SWITCH
          C  DEMONSTRATES CALLING AN ASSEMBLER SUBROUTINE
          C  DEMONSTRATES USING A FORTRAN FUNCTION
                DIMENSION TODAY(2), TITLE(12), COORD(101,2), LINE(101)
                COMMON IGLBSW
                CALL DATE(TODAY)
          C    WE DON'T HAVE THE 'DATA' STATEMENT AVAILABLE IN THIS FORTRAN.
          C    WE CAN USE THE FOLLOWING STATEMENTS TO SET THE CORRECT
          C    INTERNAL IBM MAINFRAME VALUES.  WE WOULD STILL PRINT THE SYMBOLS
          C    USING THE 'A' FORMAT CODE.
          C    AS AN ALTERNATIVE WE COULD READ IN THE SYMBOLS ON A CARD--
          C     READ (1,9) IASTR, IPLUS, IHYPH, LETRI, LETRX, LETRY, IBLNK
          C   9 FORMAT (7A1)
          C     *+-IXY
                IASTR = 1547714624
                IPLUS = 1312833600
                IHYPH = 1614823488
                LETRI = -918536128
                LETRX = -415219648
                LETRY = -398442432
                IBLNK = 1077952576
          C
          C  READ SCALES AND TITLE TO BE USED ON GRAPH
             10 READ (1,1) XAXIS, YAXIS, TITLE
          C  CHECK FOR END OF FILE
                IF (XAXIS + 1) 11,999,11
             11 IGLBSW=0
          C--CALCULATE 'X' VALUES BASED ON LENGTH OF X-AXIS
                DO 20 I = 1, 101
                  R = I - 1
                  COORD(I,1) = -(XAXIS - R * XAXIS / 50.)
             20 CONTINUE
          C--CALCULATE 'Y' VALUES FROM 'X' VALUES
                DO 30 I = 1, 101
                  X = COORD(I,1)
                  COORD(I,2) = EQU(X)
             30 CONTINUE
          C--CONVERT X,Y VALUES TO PRINT POSITIONS (X) OR LINE NUMBER (Y)
                DO 40 I = 1, 101
                  COORD(I,1) = I
                  IF (ABS(COORD(I,2)) - YAXIS) 41,41,42
             42   COORD(I,2) = 0.
                  GO TO 40
             41   Z = 40. * (COORD(I,2) / YAXIS + 1.)
                  IF (COORD(I,2)) 45,46,46
             45   N = Z + 1.49
                  GO TO 47
             46   N = Z + 1.5
             47   COORD(I,2) = 82 - N
             40 CONTINUE
          C--PRINT THE GRAPH

          09/07/75            FORTMAIN                                                    0002
          C    PRINT TITLE OR COMMENTS
                WRITE(3,2) TODAY, TITLE
          C    PRINT 'Y' AND LENGTH AT TOP OF Y-AXIS
                WRITE(3,3) LETRY, YAXIS
                DO 90 I = 1, 81
          C    INITIALIZE PRINT AREA TO BLANKS
                   DO 51 J = 1, 101
                     LINE(J) = IBLNK
             51    CONTINUE
          C    CHECK FOR X-AXIS
                  IF (I - 41) 52,53,52
             53   DO 55 J = 2, 100
                    LINE(J) = IHYPH
             55   CONTINUE
                  DO 57 J = 6, 96, 5
                    LINE(J) = IPLUS
             57   CONTINUE
                  LINE(1) = LETRX
                  LINE(101) = LETRX
             52   LINE(51) = LETRI
          C    CHECK FOR 1/2" Y-AXIS MARKERS
                  IF (MOD(I,4)-1) 60,59,60
             59   LINE(51) = IPLUS
          C    PLOT POINTS FROM EQUATION
             60   DO 70 J = 1, 101
                    T = I
                    IF (COORD(J,2) - T) 70,71,70
             71     M = COORD(J,1)
                    LINE(M) = IASTR
             70   CONTINUE
          C    IF X-AXIS, PRINT SCALES AT EACH END
                  IF (I-41) 80,81,80
             80   WRITE(3,4) LINE
                  GO TO 90
             81   XAXISM = -XAXIS
                  WRITE(3,5) XAXISM, LINE, XAXIS
             90 CONTINUE
          C    PRINT BOTTOM 'Y' ON Y-AXIS
                YAXIS = -YAXIS
                WRITE(3,3) LETRY, YAXIS
                GO TO 10
          C
            999 STOP
              1 FORMAT (2F10.0, 12A4)
              2 FORMAT (1H1, 2A4, 27X, 12A4)
              3 FORMAT (1H , 60X, A1, F10.4)
              4 FORMAT (1H , 10X, 101A1)
              5 FORMAT (1H , F9.4, 1X, 101A1, F10.4)
                END
 

          09/07/75            FORTMAIN                                                    0003

// EXEC FORTRAN
 

                               TAPE OPERATING SYSTEM/360 FORTRAN   360M-FO-409 CL 2-3

          C FUNCTION FOR F(X)
                FUNCTION EQU(X)
                DIMENSION C(8)
                COMMON IGLBSW
          C
          C FUNCTION FOR A GENERAL POLYNOMIAL
                IF (IGLBSW - 1) 11,10,11
             11 READ (1,1) C
              1 FORMAT (8F10.0)
                IGLBSW = 1
             10 X2 = X * X
                X4 = X2 * X2
                EQU = C(1) + C(2)*X + C(3)*X2 +
               -      C(4)*X2*X + C(5)*X4 +
               -      C(6)*X4*X + C(7)*X4*X2 +
               -      C(8)*X4*X2*X
          C
          C FUNCTION FOR TRIGONOMETRY
          C      T = SIN(X)
          C   OPTIONAL-MULTIPLY BY AN AMPLITUDE
          C      EQU = 4 * T
          C
                RETURN
                END
